local Player = game.Players.LocalPlayer

local FistStrength = game.Players.LocalPlayer.PrivateStats.FistStrength
local BodyToughness = game.Players.LocalPlayer.PrivateStats.BodyToughness
local MovementSpeed = game.Players.LocalPlayer.PrivateStats.MovementSpeed
local JumpForce = game.Players.LocalPlayer.PrivateStats.JumpForce
local PsychicPower = game.Players.LocalPlayer.PrivateStats.PsychicPower
local suffixes = {'','K','M','B','T','Qa','Qi'}

local function format(val)
	for i=1, #suffixes do
		if tonumber(val) < 10^(i*3) then
			return math.floor(val/((10^((i-1)*3))/100))/(100)..suffixes[i]
		end
	end
end

-- FistStrength:
SPTS.FistStrengthVal.Text = format(tonumber(FistStrength.Value))
FistStrength.Changed:Connect(function()
	local text = tostring(format(FistStrength.Value))
	for i=1,#text do
		wait(0.1)
		SPTS.FistStrengthVal.Text = string.sub(text,1,i)
	end
end)

-- Body Toughness:
SPTS.BodyToughnessVal.Text = format(tonumber(BodyToughness.Value))
BodyToughness.Changed:Connect(function()
	local text = tostring(format(BodyToughness.Value))
	for i=1,#text do
		wait(0.1)
		SPTS.BodyToughnessVal.Text = string.sub(text,1,i)
	end
end)

-- MovementSpeed:
SPTS.MovementSpeedVal.Text = format(tonumber(MovementSpeed.Value))
MovementSpeed.Changed:Connect(function()
	local text = tostring(format(MovementSpeed.Value))
	for i=1,#text do
		wait(0.1)
		SPTS.MovementSpeedVal.Text = string.sub(text,1,i)
	end
end)

-- Jump Force:
SPTS.JumpForceVal.Text = format(tonumber(JumpForce.Value))
JumpForce.Changed:Connect(function()
	local text = tostring(format(JumpForce.Value))
	for i=1,#text do
		wait(0.1)
		SPTS.JumpForceVal.Text = string.sub(text,1,i)
	end
end)

--PsychicPower
SPTS.PsychicPowerVal.Text = format(tonumber(PsychicPower.Value))
PsychicPower.Changed:Connect(function()
	local text = tostring(format(PsychicPower.Value))
	for i=1,#text do
		wait(0.1)
		SPTS.PsychicPowerVal.Text = string.sub(text,1,i)
	end
end)

		ConcealedAura = false
	end)

	SPTS.BodyToughnessMulti.Text = game.Players.LocalPlayer.PlayerGui.ScreenGui.MenuFrame.InfoFrame.BTMultiplierTxt.Text
	SPTS.MovementSpeedVal_2.Text = game.Players.LocalPlayer.PlayerGui.ScreenGui.MenuFrame.InfoFrame.MSMultiplierTxt.Text
	SPTS.JumpForceVal_2.Text = game.Players.LocalPlayer.PlayerGui.ScreenGui.MenuFrame.InfoFrame.JFMultiplierTxt.Text
	SPTS.PsychicPowerVal_2.Text = game.Players.LocalPlayer.PlayerGui.ScreenGui.MenuFrame.InfoFrame.PPMultiplierTxt.Text
	SPTS.TokensVal.Text = "Tokens: "..game.Players.LocalPlayer.PrivateStats.Token.Value

	if AutoConcealAura == true then
		if ConcealedAura == false then
			local args = {
				[1] = {
					[1] = "ConcealRevealAura"
				}
			}

			game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").RemoteEvent:FireServer(unpack(args))
			ConcealedAura = true
		end
	end

		if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.Health == 0 then
			local args = {
				[1] = {
					[1] = "Respawn"
				}
			}

			game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").RemoteEvent:FireServer(unpack(args))
			wait(5)
			game.Players.LocalPlayer.PlayerGui.IntroGui.Enabled = false
			game.Lighting.Blur.Enabled = false
			game.Players.LocalPlayer.PlayerGui.ScreenGui.Enabled = true
			wait(2)
			BreakHum = false
			Died = false
			ConcealedAura = false
		end
	end
